<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Choral Preludes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Wilhelm_Friedemann" title="Category:Bach, Wilhelm Friedemann">Bach, Wilhelm Friedemann</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IWB 5
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>7 Chorals
<ol><li>Nun kommt, der Heiden Heiland
</li><li>Christe, der du bist Tag und Licht
</li><li>Jesu, meine Freude
</li><li>Durch Adams Fall ist ganz verderbt
</li><li>Wir danken dir, Herr Jesu Christ
</li><li>Was Mein Gott will
</li><li>Wir Christen leut!
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>Organ
</td></tr></table>
